### `BatchSelector.tsx`

This is the main UI. Uses Popover + Command + AlertDialog. Each row has:
- Filename
- Active indicator (Badge)
- "Aktif yap" button (or checkmark if already active)
- "Sil" button → opens AlertDialog

```tsx
"use client";

import { useMemo, useState } from "react";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { Command, CommandInput, CommandList, CommandItem } from "@/components/ui/command";
import { Popover, PopoverTrigger, PopoverContent } from "@/components/ui/popover";
import {
  AlertDialog, AlertDialogContent, AlertDialogHeader, AlertDialogTitle, AlertDialogDescription,
  AlertDialogFooter, AlertDialogCancel, AlertDialogAction,
} from "@/components/ui/alert-dialog";
import { useToast } from "@/components/ui/toast";
import { useActiveBatch, useBatches, useActivateBatch, useDeleteBatch } from "./useBatch";
import { Check, ChevronDown, Trash2 } from "lucide-react";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

export function BatchSelector() {
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  const [confirmDelete, setConfirmDelete] = useState<number | null>(null);
  const batches = useBatches();
  const active = useActiveBatch();
  const activate = useActivateBatch();
  const remove = useDeleteBatch();
  const toast = useToast();

  const activeBatch = active.data;
  const list = batches.data ?? [];
  const confirmTarget = list.find((b) => b.id === confirmDelete) ?? null;

  const onActivate = (id: number) => {
    activate.mutate(id, {
      onSuccess: (b) => {
        toast.push({ tone: "success", title: "Aktif batch güncellendi", description: b.filename });
        setOpen(false);
      },
      onError: () => toast.push({ tone: "destructive", title: "Aktif batch güncellenemedi" }),
    });
  };

  const onConfirmDelete = () => {
    if (!confirmTarget) return;
    const name = confirmTarget.filename;
    remove.mutate(confirmTarget.id, {
      onSuccess: () => toast.push({ tone: "success", title: "Batch silindi", description: name }),
      onError: () => toast.push({ tone: "destructive", title: "Batch silinemedi" }),
    });
  };

  return (
    <>
      <Popover open={open} onOpenChange={setOpen}>
        <PopoverTrigger>
          <Button variant="outline" className="w-[280px] justify-between">
            <span className="truncate">
              {activeBatch ? activeBatch.filename : "Batch seçin"}
            </span>
            <ChevronDown className="h-4 w-4 shrink-0 opacity-60" />
          </Button>
        </PopoverTrigger>
        <PopoverContent className="w-[360px] p-0">
          <Command>
            <CommandInput placeholder="Batch ara..." />
            <CommandList>
              {list.length === 0 ? (
                <div className="px-3 py-6 text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                  Henüz batch yok
                </div>
              ) : (
                list.map((b) => (
                  <CommandItem
                    key={b.id}
                    value={`${b.filename} ${b.id}`}
                    onSelect={() => onActivate(b.id)}
                  >
                    <div className="flex w-full items-center gap-2">
                      <div className="flex flex-1 flex-col items-start">
                        <div className="flex w-full items-center gap-2">
                          <span className="truncate text-sm font-medium">{b.filename}</span>
                          {b.is_active ? (
                            <Badge tone="success" className="shrink-0">Aktif</Badge>
                          ) : null}
                        </div>
                        <span className="font-mono text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                          {b.imported_rows}/{b.total_rows} satır · {b.status}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      <Button
                        size="icon"
                        variant="ghost"
                        onClick={(e) => {
                          e.stopPropagation();
                          setConfirmDelete(b.id);
                        }}
                        aria-label="Sil"
                      >
                        <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4" />
                      </Button>
                    </div>
                  </CommandItem>
                ))
              )}
            </CommandList>
          </Command>
        </PopoverContent>
      </Popover>

      <AlertDialog open={confirmDelete !== null} onOpenChange={(v) => !v && setConfirmDelete(null)}>
        <AlertDialogContent>
          <AlertDialogHeader>
            <AlertDialogTitle>Batch silinsin mi?</AlertDialogTitle>
            <AlertDialogDescription>
              <span className="font-mono">{confirmTarget?.filename}</span> ve tüm kayıtları (validasyon/düzeltme dahil) kalıcı olarak silinir. Bu işlem geri alınamaz.
            </AlertDialogDescription>
          </AlertDialogHeader>
          <AlertDialogFooter>
            <AlertDialogCancel>İptal</AlertDialogCancel>
            <AlertDialogAction onClick={onConfirmDelete} variant="destructive">Sil</AlertDialogAction>
          </AlertDialogFooter>
        </AlertDialogContent>
      </AlertDialog>
    </>
  );
}
```

Hmm wait — `PopoverTrigger` is wrapped around a `<Button>`. With my design where PopoverTrigger just renders a button (not asChild), the button structure is `<button><button>...</button></button>`. That's invalid HTML.

Let me re-think. Two options:
1. PopoverTrigger doesn't render a button, just clones the child.
2. PopoverTrigger is the trigger element, the trigger is identified via ref.

For asChild approach, I need to clone the child element. The Button component accepts onClick and ref.

Let me simplify: PopoverTrigger expects children to be a single React element (typically a Button), and clones it to add onClick + ref. This is the standard shadcn pattern.

```tsx
export function PopoverTrigger({ children, className }: { children: React.ReactElement; className?: string }) {
  const ctx = usePopover();
  const child = children as React.ReactElement<{
    onClick?: (e: React.MouseEvent) => void;
    ref?: React.Ref<HTMLElement>;
  }>;
  return React.cloneElement(child, {
    onClick: (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
      child.props.onClick?.(e);
      ctx.setOpen(!ctx.open);
    },
    ref: (node: HTMLElement | null) => {
      (ctx.triggerRef as React.MutableRefObject<HTMLElement | null>).current = node;
    },
    className: cn(child.props.className, className),
  });
}
```

But Button is `React.forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>`, so passing ref should work.

OK let me also think: the child already has an onClick from Button. cloneElement will OVERRIDE the existing onClick (replace it with the new one). To preserve the existing onClick, I need to call it manually — which I do in the wrapped function above. Good.

Now for the actual usage:
```tsx
<PopoverTrigger>
  <Button variant="outline">...</Button>
</PopoverTrigger>
```

This clones the Button, adds onClick+ref. ✓

### `ImportDropzone.tsx`

```tsx
"use client";

import { useRef, useState } from "react";
import { Upload, Loader2 } from "lucide-react";
import { Card, CardContent } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { useToast } from "@/components/ui/toast";
import { useImportCsv, useActivateBatch } from "./useBatch";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

export function ImportDropzone() {
  const [dragging, setDragging] = useState(false);
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
  const upload = useImportCsv();
  const activate = useActivateBatch();
  const toast = useToast();

  const handleFile = async (file: File) => {
    if (!file.name.toLowerCase().endsWith(".csv")) {
      toast.push({ tone: "warning", title: "Sadece CSV dosyaları desteklenir" });
      return;
    }
    const fd = new FormData();
    fd.append("file", file);
    try {
      const result = await upload.mutateAsync(fd);
      await activate.mutateAsync(result.batch_id);
      toast.push({
        tone: "success",
        title: "İçe aktarıldı",
        description: `${result.filename} · ${result.imported_rows}/${result.total_rows} satır · ${result.elapsed_ms}ms`,
      });
    } catch {
      toast.push({ tone: "destructive", title: "İçe aktarma başarısız" });
    }
  };

  return (
    <Card
      onDragOver={(e) => { e.preventDefault(); setDragging(true); }}
      onDragLeave={() => setDragging(false)}
      onDrop={(e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        setDragging(false);
        const file = e.dataTransfer.files?.[0];
        if (file) void handleFile(file);
      }}
      className={cn(
        "border-dashed transition-colors",
        dragging ? "border-primary bg-accent" : "border-border",
        upload.isPending && "pointer-events-none opacity-60"
      )}
    >
      <CardContent className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-3 py-10">
        {upload.isPending || activate.isPending ? (
          <Loader2 className="h-8 w-8 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
        ) : (
          <Upload className="h-8 w-8 text-muted-foreground" />
        )}
        <div className="text-center">
          <p className="text-sm font-medium">
            CSV dosyasını sürükle ya da seç
          </p>
          <p className="mt-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            Yüklendikten sonra otomatik aktif batch olur.
          </p>
        </div>
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          size="sm"
          onClick={() => inputRef.current?.click()}
          disabled={upload.isPending}
        >
          Dosya Seç
        </Button>
        <input
          ref={inputRef}
          type="file"
          accept=".csv,text/csv"
          className="hidden"
          onChange={(e) => {
            const file = e.target.files?.[0];
            if (file) void handleFile(file);
            e.target.value = "";
          }}
        />
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}
```

### `ImportPage.tsx`

```tsx
"use client";

import { useEffect, useRef } from "react";
import { usePathname, useRouter, useSearchParams } from "next/navigation";
import { BatchSelector } from "./BatchSelector";
import { ImportDropzone } from "./ImportDropzone";
import { useActiveBatch, useActivateBatch } from "./useBatch";

export function ImportPage() {
  const searchParams = useSearchParams();
  const router = useRouter();
  const pathname = usePathname();
  const active = useActiveBatch();
  const activate = useActivateBatch();
  const hydratedRef = useRef(false);

  // URL → server: mount'ta URL'deki batch_id farklıysa aktif et
  useEffect(() => {
    if (hydratedRef.current) return;
    hydratedRef.current = true;
    const urlId = searchParams?.get("batch_id");
    if (!urlId) return;
    const numId = Number(urlId);
    if (!Number.isFinite(numId)) return;
    if (active.data && active.data.id === numId) return;
    activate.mutate(numId);
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, []);

  // server → URL: aktif batch değişince URL'i güncelle
  useEffect(() => {
    const urlId = searchParams?.get("batch_id") ?? null;
    const activeId = active.data?.id != null ? String(active.data.id) : null;
    if (urlId === activeId) return;
    const url = activeId ? `${pathname}?batch_id=${activeId}` : pathname;
    router.replace(url, { scroll: false });
  }, [active.data, pathname, router, searchParams]);

  return (
    <main className="container mx-auto space-y-4 py-8">
      <header className="flex items-end justify-between">
        <div>
          <p className="font-mono text-sm text-muted-foreground">MAGNA · Import</p>
          <h1 className="mt-1 text-3xl font-bold tracking-tight">CSV Import</h1>
        </div>
        <BatchSelector />
      </header>

      <ImportDropzone />
    </main>
  );
}
```

Actually, since we want a single `useBatch.ts` with all hooks co-located, and we need the active batch query accessible from shared, the simplest is:

`src/hooks/useActiveBatch.ts` (shared):
```ts
"use client";
import { useQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { api } from "@/lib/api";
import { queryKeys } from "@/lib/query-keys";

export interface ActiveBatch {
  id: number;
  filename: string;
  file_hash: string;
  uploaded_at: string;
  total_rows: number;
  imported_rows: number;
  status: string;
  is_active: boolean;
}

export function useActiveBatch() {
  return useQuery({
    queryKey: queryKeys.imports.activeBatch,
    queryFn: () => api.get<ActiveBatch | null>("/api/v1/imports/batches/active"),
  });
}
```

`features/import/useBatch.ts` (feature):
```ts
"use client";
import { useMutation, useQuery, useQueryClient } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { api } from "@/lib/api";
import { queryKeys } from "@/lib/query-keys";
import { useActiveBatch, type ActiveBatch } from "@/hooks/useActiveBatch";
import type { BatchOut, ImportSummary } from "./types";

export { useActiveBatch };
export type { ActiveBatch };

export function useBatches() {
  return useQuery({ ... });
}

export function useActivateBatch() { ... }
export function useDeleteBatch() { ... }
export function useImportCsv() { ... }
```

This re-export pattern keeps the feature's public API complete while satisfying boundaries.

Now let me think about edge cases:

1. **The Popover's `asChild` pattern with the Button:** The Button component is `React.forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>`. cloneElement with onClick+ref should work. But TypeScript will complain about the ref type. Let me handle it with type assertions.

2. **Ref types in PopoverTrigger:** The Button ref is `HTMLButtonElement`. The popover stores `HTMLElement`. Should be compatible.

3. **Click-outside detection:** When clicking inside PopoverContent, `ref.current.contains(t)` should be true. When clicking on the trigger button, `triggerRef.current?.contains(t)` should be true (skip). Otherwise, close.

4. **The Button inside PopoverContent (Trash icon):** When clicked, it shouldn't trigger the parent CommandItem's onClick. I use `e.stopPropagation()` to prevent this. But the parent CommandItem is a `<button>`, so nesting `<button>` inside is invalid HTML!

Hmm, this is a problem. CommandItem renders a `<button>`, and the Trash button is nested inside. That's invalid HTML.

Solutions:
- Don't use a button for CommandItem — use a div with role="option" and tabIndex.
- Don't use a button for the trash icon — use a span with onClick and role="button" (still not ideal for keyboard).
- The CommandItem doesn't have a button wrapper; the user clicks anywhere on the row, and the trash is a separate sibling.

Let me refactor: CommandItem renders a `<div role="option">` with onClick. The trash icon is a separate `<button>` as a sibling (positioned absolutely or via flex).

```tsx
export function CommandItem({ value, onSelect, children, className }) {
  ...
  return (
    <div
      role="option"
      aria-selected={false}
      onClick={onSelect}
      onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === "Enter" || e.key === " ") { e.preventDefault(); onSelect?.(); }}}
      tabIndex={0}
      className={cn("flex w-full cursor-pointer items-center gap-2 rounded-sm px-2 py-1.5 text-sm hover:bg-accent", className)}
    >
      {children}
    </div>
  );
}
```

This way, the children can include other buttons (like the trash) without nesting.

5. **The Trash button's stopPropagation:** since the parent is a div (not a button), stopPropagation isn't strictly needed, but I should still call it to be safe in case the click bubbles up to other elements.

Actually with onClick on the div, the trash button's onClick fires first (event.target is the button), and bubbles up to the div's onClick. We need stopPropagation to prevent the row's onClick from firing.

```tsx
<Button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); setConfirmDelete(b.id); }}>...</Button>
```

Yes, stopPropagation is needed.

6. **The CommandItem keyboard accessibility:** `role="option"` requires the parent to have `role="listbox"`. CommandList should have `role="listbox"`. And the input should have `aria-controls` pointing to the list.

For simplicity, I'll skip strict ARIA and rely on native divs with onClick. The user didn't require strict accessibility. But I'll add `role="option"` and `role="listbox"` for basic correctness.

7. **Stop event propagation on Trash button:** I need this so the CommandItem onClick doesn't fire when clicking the trash.

OK I think the design is solid. Let me also think about the lucide icons:
- `Check` for active indicator
- `ChevronDown` for the dropdown trigger
- `Trash2` for delete
- `Upload` for the dropzone
- `Loader2` for loading
- `Search` for command input

These are all in lucide-react. Good.

### Let me also verify the URL sync logic:

Mount with `?batch_id=3`:
1. `hydratedRef.current = false`
2. `useActiveBatch` fires, returns null (no active yet, or different active)
3. First effect runs: `hydratedRef.current = false`, sets to true, reads `urlId="3"`, active is null, calls `activate.mutate(3)`.
4. `activate.mutate(3)` invalidates `queryKeys.imports.all`, refetches `useActiveBatch`, returns batch 3.
5. Second effect runs: `urlId="3"`, `activeId="3"`, no change.

Mount with `?batch_id=3` and active=5:
1. `useActiveBatch` returns batch 5.
2. First effect: `hydratedRef.current = false`, sets to true, reads `urlId="3"`, active is 5, `5 !== 3`, calls `activate.mutate(3)`.
3. Active becomes 3.
4. Second effect: `urlId="3"`, `activeId="3"`, no change.

Mount with no `?batch_id`, active=5:
1. `useActiveBatch` returns 5.
2. First effect: `hydratedRef.current = false`, sets to true, reads `urlId=null`, skip.
3. Second effect: `urlId=null`, `activeId="5"`, URL becomes `?batch_id=5`.

Mount with `?batch_id=3` and active=3:
1. `useActiveBatch` returns 3.
2. First effect: `hydratedRef.current = false`, sets to true, reads `urlId="3"`, active is 3, `3 === 3`, skip.
3. Second effect: `urlId="3"`, `activeId="3"`, no change.

After clicking activate(7):
1. `activate.mutate(7)` → server sets active=7, invalidates `queryKeys.imports.all`.
2. `useActiveBatch` refetches, returns 7.
3. Second effect: `urlId="3"`, `activeId="7"`, URL becomes `?batch_id=7`.

After deleting active batch (batch 3):
1. `useDeleteBatch.mutate(3)` → server deletes batch 3, AppSetting cleared.
2. `useActiveBatch` refetches, returns null.
3. Second effect: `urlId="3"`, `activeId=null`, URL becomes `/import` (no query).

Wait, but the URL is `/import?batch_id=3`. After delete, active is null, URL should be `/import`. My code:
```ts
const url = activeId ? `${pathname}?batch_id=${activeId}` : pathname;
```
If `activeId` is null, `url = pathname` = `/import`. ✓

But wait — there's an issue. The active batch is now deleted, but `useBatches` refetches and returns the remaining batches (e.g., batch 1 and 2). In the BatchSelector, the user sees these but the active badge is gone (since active is null). The user can re-activate by clicking.

OK this design works.

```json
"no-restricted-imports": [

      }
    ]
  }
]
```

So no `@/features/import/BatchSelector` deep imports. Must use `@/features/import` (the barrel).

### Now let me also think about the api client `delete` method:

```ts
export const api = {
  get: <T>(path: string) => apiFetch<T>(path),
  post: <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) => apiFetch<T>(path, { method: "POST", body }),
  patch: <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) => apiFetch<T>(path, { method: "PATCH", body }),
  upload: <T>(path: string, form: FormData) => apiFetch<T>(path, { method: "POST", body: form }),
};
```

Adding:
```ts
delete: <T>(path: string) => apiFetch<T>(path, { method: "DELETE" }),
```

The backend returns 204 No Content for DELETE, with empty body. `apiFetch` tries to parse as JSON. If body is empty, `await res.text()` returns empty string, which is then `data as T` (void). Should work.

Wait, looking more carefully:
```ts
const isJson = res.headers.get("content-type")?.includes("application/json");
const data = isJson ? await res.json() : await res.text();
```

For 204, content-type is typically empty or `text/plain`. So `data = ""`. `data as T` where T is `void` is `"" as void`. Should be fine.

Actually, for type safety, I could do:
```ts
delete: <T = void>(path: string) => apiFetch<T>(path, { method: "DELETE" }),
```

Or just have the caller pass the type:
```ts
api.delete<void>(`/api/v1/imports/batches/${id}`)
```

The caller can pass `<void>` explicitly. That's cleaner.

### Let me also handle the upload case more carefully

The backend's `import_file` endpoint:
```python
@router.post("/import", response_model=ImportSummary)
def import_file(
    file: UploadFile = File(...),
    db: Session = Depends(get_db),
) -> ImportSummary:
```

The form field is named `file`. So `fd.append("file", file)`. ✓

```ts
"use client";

import { useQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { api } from "@/lib/api";
import { queryKeys } from "@/lib/query-keys";

export interface ActiveBatch {
  id: number;
  filename: string;
  file_hash: string;
  uploaded_at: string;
  total_rows: number;
  imported_rows: number;
  status: string;
  is_active: boolean;
}

export function useActiveBatch() {
  return useQuery({
    queryKey: queryKeys.imports.activeBatch,
    queryFn: () => api.get<ActiveBatch | null>("/api/v1/imports/batches/active"),
  });
}
```

# FILE: apps/web/src/components/ui/popover.tsx

```tsx
"use client";

import * as React from "react";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

interface PopoverContextValue {
  open: boolean;
  setOpen: (next: boolean) => void;
  triggerRef: React.MutableRefObject<HTMLElement | null>;
}

const PopoverCtx = React.createContext<PopoverContextValue | null>(null);

function usePopoverCtx(): PopoverContextValue {
  const ctx = React.useContext(PopoverCtx);
  if (!ctx) throw new Error("Popover bileşenleri <Popover> içinde olmalı");
  return ctx;
}

export interface PopoverProps {
  open?: boolean;
  onOpenChange?: (next: boolean) => void;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

export function Popover({ open, onOpenChange, children }: PopoverProps) {
  const [internal, setInternal] = React.useState(false);
  const triggerRef = React.useRef<HTMLElement | null>(null);
  const isControlled = open !== undefined;
  const current = isControlled ? open : internal;
  const setOpen = React.useCallback(
    (next: boolean) => {
      onOpenChange?.(next);
      if (!isControlled) setInternal(next);
    },
    [isControlled, onOpenChange],
  );
  return (
    <PopoverCtx.Provider value={{ open: current, setOpen, triggerRef }}>
      <div className="relative inline-block">{children}</div>
    </PopoverCtx.Provider>
  );
}

export interface PopoverTriggerProps {
  children: React.ReactElement;
  className?: string;
}

export function PopoverTrigger({ children, className }: PopoverTriggerProps) {
  const ctx = usePopoverCtx();
  type ChildProps = { onClick?: (e: React.MouseEvent) => void; ref?: React.Ref<HTMLElement>; className?: string };
  const child = children as React.ReactElement<ChildProps>;
  const original = child.props;
  return React.cloneElement(child, {
    onClick: (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
      original.onClick?.(e);
      ctx.setOpen(!ctx.open);
    },
    ref: (node: HTMLElement | null) => {
      ctx.triggerRef.current = node;
    },
    className: cn(original.className, className),
  });
}

export interface PopoverContentProps {
  className?: string;
  align?: "start" | "end" | "center";
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

export function PopoverContent({ className, align = "start", children }: PopoverContentProps) {
  const ctx = usePopoverCtx();
  const ref = React.useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (!ctx.open) return;
    const onDown = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      const target = e.target as Node;
      if (ref.current?.contains(target)) return;
      if (ctx.triggerRef.current?.contains(target)) return;
      ctx.setOpen(false);
    };
    const onKey = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
      if (e.key === "Escape") ctx.setOpen(false);
    };
    document.addEventListener("mousedown", onDown);
    document.addEventListener("keydown", onKey);
    return () => {
      document.removeEventListener("mousedown", onDown);
      document.removeEventListener("keydown", onKey);
    };
  }, [ctx]);
  if (!ctx.open) return null;
  const alignClass =
    align === "end" ? "right-0" : align === "center" ? "left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2" : "left-0";
  return (
    <div
      ref={ref}
      role="dialog"
      className={cn(
        "absolute top-full z-50 mt-1 min-w-[280px] rounded-md border bg-popover p-2 text-popover-foreground shadow-md",
        alignClass,
        className,
      )}
    >
      {children}
    </div>
  );
}
```

# FILE: apps/web/src/components/ui/command.tsx

```tsx
"use client";

import * as React from "react";
import { Search } from "lucide-react";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

interface CommandContextValue {
  query: string;
  setQuery: (q: string) => void;
}

const CommandCtx = React.createContext<CommandContextValue | null>(null);

function useCommandCtx(): CommandContextValue {
  const ctx = React.useContext(CommandCtx);
  if (!ctx) throw new Error("Command bileşenleri <Command> içinde olmalı");
  return ctx;
}

export function Command({ children, className }: { children: React.ReactNode; className?: string }) {
  const [query, setQuery] = React.useState("");
  return (
    <CommandCtx.Provider value={{ query, setQuery }}>
      <div className={cn("flex flex-col", className)}>{children}</div>
    </CommandCtx.Provider>
  );
}

export function CommandInput({ className, placeholder }: { className?: string; placeholder?: string }) {
  const ctx = useCommandCtx();
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 border-b px-2">
      <Search className="h-4 w-4 shrink-0 text-muted-foreground" />
      <input
        value={ctx.query}
        onChange={(e) => ctx.setQuery(e.target.value)}
        placeholder={placeholder}
        className={cn(
          "flex h-9 w-full bg-transparent py-1 text-sm outline-none placeholder:text-muted-foreground",
          className,
        )}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

export function CommandList({ children, className }: { children: React.ReactNode; className?: string }) {
  return (
    <div role="listbox" className={cn("max-h-[300px] overflow-y-auto p-1", className)}>
      {children}
    </div>
  );
}

export interface CommandItemProps {
  value: string;
  onSelect?: () => void;
  children: React.ReactNode;
  className?: string;
}

export function CommandItem({ value, onSelect, children, className }: CommandItemProps) {
  const ctx = useCommandCtx();
  const matches = ctx.query === "" || value.toLowerCase().includes(ctx.query.toLowerCase());
  if (!matches) return null;
  return (
    <div
      role="option"
      aria-selected={false}
      tabIndex={0}
      onClick={onSelect}
      onKeyDown={(e) => {
        if (e.key === "Enter" || e.key === " ") {
          e.preventDefault();
          onSelect?.();
        }
      }}
      className={cn(
        "flex w-full cursor-pointer items-center gap-2 rounded-sm px-2 py-1.5 text-sm outline-none hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground focus-visible:bg-accent",
        className,
      )}
    >
      {children}
    </div>
  );
}

export function CommandGroup({
  children,
  heading,
  className,
}: {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  heading?: string;
  className?: string;
}) {
  return (
    <div className={cn("py-1", className)}>
      {heading ? (
        <div className="px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground">{heading}</div>
      ) : null}
      {children}
    </div>
  );
}
```

# FILE: apps/web/src/components/ui/alert-dialog.tsx

```tsx
"use client";

import * as React from "react";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";

interface AlertDialogContextValue {
  open: boolean;
  setOpen: (next: boolean) => void;
}

const AlertDialogCtx = React.createContext<AlertDialogContextValue | null>(null);

function useAlertDialogCtx(): AlertDialogContextValue {
  const ctx = React.useContext(AlertDialogCtx);
  if (!ctx) throw new Error("AlertDialog bileşenleri <AlertDialog> içinde olmalı");
  return ctx;
}

export interface AlertDialogProps {
  open?: boolean;
  onOpenChange?: (next: boolean) => void;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

export function AlertDialog({ open, onOpenChange, children }: AlertDialogProps) {
  const [internal, setInternal] = React.useState(false);
  const isControlled = open !== undefined;
  const current = isControlled ? open : internal;
  const setOpen = React.useCallback(
    (next: boolean) => {
      onOpenChange?.(next);
      if (!isControlled) setInternal(next);
    },
    [isControlled, onOpenChange],
  );
  return <AlertDialogCtx.Provider value={{ open: current, setOpen }}>{children}</AlertDialogCtx.Provider>;
}

export function AlertDialogContent({
  className,
  children,
}: {
  className?: string;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}) {
  const ctx = useAlertDialogCtx();
  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (!ctx.open) return;
    const onKey = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
      if (e.key === "Escape") ctx.setOpen(false);
    };
    document.addEventListener("keydown", onKey);
    return () => document.removeEventListener("keydown", onKey);
  }, [ctx]);
  if (!ctx.open) return null;
  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center">
      <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/60" aria-hidden onClick={() => ctx.setOpen(false)} />
      <div
        role="alertdialog"
        aria-modal="true"
        className={cn(
          "relative z-10 w-full max-w-md rounded-lg border bg-card p-6 text-card-foreground shadow-lg",
          className,
        )}
      >
        {children}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function AlertDialogHeader({
  className,
  children,
}: {
  className?: string;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}) {
  return <div className={cn("mb-4 flex flex-col gap-1", className)}>{children}</div>;
}

export function AlertDialogTitle({
  className,
  children,
}: {
  className?: string;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}) {
  return <h2 className={cn("text-lg font-semibold", className)}>{children}</h2>;
}

export function AlertDialogDescription({
  className,
  children,
}: {
  className?: string;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}) {
  return <p className={cn("text-sm text-muted-foreground", className)}>{children}</p>;
}

export function AlertDialogFooter({
  className,
  children,
}: {
  className?: string;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}) {
  return <div className={cn("mt-4 flex justify-end gap-2", className)}>{children}</div>;
}

export function AlertDialogCancel({
  children,
  onClick,
}: {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  onClick?: () => void;
}) {
  const ctx = useAlertDialogCtx();
  return (
    <Button
      variant="outline"
      onClick={() => {
        onClick?.();
        ctx.setOpen(false);
      }}
    >
      {children}
    </Button>
  );
}

export function AlertDialogAction({
  children,
  onClick,
  variant = "destructive",
}: {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  onClick?: () => void;
  variant?: "default" | "destructive";
}) {
  const ctx = useAlertDialogCtx();
  return (
    <Button
      variant={variant}
      onClick={() => {
        onClick?.();
        ctx.setOpen(false);
      }}
    >
      {children}
    </Button>
  );
}
```

```ts
export interface BatchOut {
  id: number;
  filename: string;
  file_hash: string;
  uploaded_at: string;
  total_rows: number;
  imported_rows: number;
  status: string;
  is_active: boolean;
}

export interface ImportSummary {
  batch_id: number;
  filename: string;
  file_hash: string;
  total_rows: number;
  imported_rows: number;
  duplicate_file: boolean;
  duplicate_row_skipped: number;
  parse_failed_count: number;
  failed_rows_sample: Array<Record<string, string>>;
  status: string;
  elapsed_ms: number;
}
```

# FILE: apps/web/src/features/import/useBatch.ts

```ts
"use client";

import { useMutation, useQuery, useQueryClient } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { api } from "@/lib/api";
import { queryKeys } from "@/lib/query-keys";
import { useActiveBatch, type ActiveBatch } from "@/hooks/useActiveBatch";
import type { BatchOut, ImportSummary } from "./types";

export { useActiveBatch };
export type { ActiveBatch };

export function useBatches() {
  return useQuery({
    queryKey: queryKeys.imports.batches,
    queryFn: () => api.get<BatchOut[]>("/api/v1/imports/batches"),
  });
}

export function useActivateBatch() {
  const qc = useQueryClient();
  return useMutation({
    mutationFn: (batchId: number) =>
      api.post<BatchOut>(`/api/v1/imports/batches/${batchId}/activate`),
    onSuccess: async () => {
      await qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.imports.all });
    },
  });
}

export function useDeleteBatch() {
  const qc = useQueryClient();
  return useMutation({
    mutationFn: (batchId: number) =>
      api.delete<void>(`/api/v1/imports/batches/${batchId}`),
    onSuccess: async () => {
      await qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.imports.all });
    },
  });
}

export function useImportCsv() {
  const qc = useQueryClient();
  return useMutation({
    mutationFn: (form: FormData) =>
      api.upload<ImportSummary>("/api/v1/imports/import", form),
    onSuccess: async () => {
      await qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.imports.all });
    },
  });
}
```

---

# FILE: apps/web/src/features/import/BatchSelector.tsx

```tsx
"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { Check, ChevronDown, Trash2 } from "lucide-react";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Command, CommandInput, CommandList, CommandItem } from "@/components/ui/command";
import { Popover, PopoverTrigger, PopoverContent } from "@/components/ui/popover";
import {
  AlertDialog,
  AlertDialogContent,
  AlertDialogDescription,
  AlertDialogFooter,
  AlertDialogHeader,
  AlertDialogTitle,
  AlertDialogAction,
  AlertDialogCancel,
} from "@/components/ui/alert-dialog";
import { useToast } from "@/components/ui/toast";
import {
  useActiveBatch,
  useBatches,
  useActivateBatch,
  useDeleteBatch,
} from "./useBatch";

export function BatchSelector() {
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  const [confirmDelete, setConfirmDelete] = useState<number | null>(null);
  const batches = useBatches();
  const active = useActiveBatch();
  const activate = useActivateBatch();
  const remove = useDeleteBatch();
  const toast = useToast();

  const list = batches.data ?? [];
  const confirmTarget = list.find((b) => b.id === confirmDelete) ?? null;

  const onActivate = (id: number) => {
    activate.mutate(id, {
      onSuccess: (b) => {
        toast.push({
          tone: "success",
          title: "Aktif batch güncellendi",
          description: b.filename,
        });
        setOpen(false);
      },
      onError: () =>
        toast.push({ tone: "destructive", title: "Aktif batch güncellenemedi" }),
    });
  };

  const onConfirmDelete = () => {
    if (!confirmTarget) return;
    const name = confirmTarget.filename;
    remove.mutate(confirmTarget.id, {
      onSuccess: () =>
        toast.push({ tone: "success", title: "Batch silindi", description: name }),
      onError: () => toast.push({ tone: "destructive", title: "Batch silinemedi" }),
    });
  };

  return (
    <>
      <Popover open={open} onOpenChange={setOpen}>
        <PopoverTrigger>
          <Button variant="outline" className="w-[300px] justify-between gap-2">
            <span className="flex items-center gap-2 truncate">
              {active.data ? (
                <>
                  <Check className="h-3.5 w-3.5 shrink-0 text-oee-good" />
                  <span className="truncate">{active.data.filename}</span>
                </>
              ) : (
                <span className="text-muted-foreground">Batch seçin</span>
              )}
            </span>
            <ChevronDown className="h-4 w-4 shrink-0 opacity-60" />
          </Button>
        </PopoverTrigger>
        <PopoverContent align="end" className="w-[400px] p-0">
          <Command>
            <CommandInput placeholder="Batch ara…" />
            <CommandList>
              {list.length === 0 ? (
                <div className="px-3 py-6 text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                  Henüz batch yok
                </div>
              ) : (
                list.map((b) => (
                  <CommandItem
                    key={b.id}
                    value={`${b.filename} ${b.id}`}
                    onSelect={() => onActivate(b.id)}
                  >
                    <div className="flex w-full items-center gap-2">
                      <div className="flex flex-1 flex-col items-start overflow-hidden">
                        <div className="flex w-full items-center gap-2">
                          <span className="truncate text-sm font-medium">
                            {b.filename}
                          </span>
                          {b.is_active ? (
                            <Badge tone="success" className="shrink-0">
                              Aktif
                            </Badge>
                          ) : null}
                        </div>
                        <span className="font-mono text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                          {b.imported_rows}/{b.total_rows} satır · {b.status}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      <Button
                        size="icon"
                        variant="ghost"
                        onClick={(e) => {
                          e.stopPropagation();
                          setConfirmDelete(b.id);
                        }}
                        aria-label="Sil"
                      >
                        <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4" />
                      </Button>
                    </div>
                  </CommandItem>
                ))
              )}
            </CommandList>
          </Command>
        </PopoverContent>
      </Popover>

      <AlertDialog
        open={confirmDelete !== null}
        onOpenChange={(next) => {
          if (!next) setConfirmDelete(null);
        }}
      >
        <AlertDialogContent>
          <AlertDialogHeader>
            <AlertDialogTitle>Batch silinsin mi?</AlertDialogTitle>
            <AlertDialogDescription>
              <span className="font-mono">{confirmTarget?.filename ?? ""}</span>{" "}
              ve tüm kayıtları (validasyon/düzeltme dahil) kalıcı olarak silinir. Bu
              işlem geri alınamaz.
            </AlertDialogDescription>
          </AlertDialogHeader>
          <AlertDialogFooter>
            <AlertDialogCancel>İptal</AlertDialogCancel>
            <AlertDialogAction onClick={onConfirmDelete}>Sil</AlertDialogAction>
          </AlertDialogFooter>
        </AlertDialogContent>
      </AlertDialog>
    </>
  );
}
```

# FILE: apps/web/src/features/import/ImportDropzone.tsx

```tsx
"use client";

import { useRef, useState } from "react";
import { Loader2, Upload } from "lucide-react";
import { Card, CardContent } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { useToast } from "@/components/ui/toast";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
import { useActivateBatch, useImportCsv } from "./useBatch";

export function ImportDropzone() {
  const [dragging, setDragging] = useState(false);
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
  const upload = useImportCsv();
  const activate = useActivateBatch();
  const toast = useToast();

  const handleFile = async (file: File) => {
    if (!file.name.toLowerCase().endsWith(".csv")) {
      toast.push({ tone: "warning", title: "Sadece CSV dosyaları desteklenir" });
      return;
    }
    const form = new FormData();
    form.append("file", file);
    try {
      const result = await upload.mutateAsync(form);
      await activate.mutateAsync(result.batch_id);
      toast.push({
        tone: "success",
        title: "İçe aktarıldı",
        description: `${result.filename} · ${result.imported_rows}/${result.total_rows} satır · ${result.elapsed_ms}ms`,
      });
    } catch {
      toast.push({ tone: "destructive", title: "İçe aktarma başarısız" });
    }
  };

  const busy = upload.isPending || activate.isPending;

  return (
    <Card
      onDragOver={(e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        if (!dragging) setDragging(true);
      }}
      onDragLeave={() => setDragging(false)}
      onDrop={(e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        setDragging(false);
        const file = e.dataTransfer.files?.[0];
        if (file) void handleFile(file);
      }}
      className={cn(
        "border-dashed transition-colors",
        dragging ? "border-primary bg-accent" : "border-border",
        busy && "pointer-events-none opacity-60",
      )}
    >
      <CardContent className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-3 py-10">
        {busy ? (
          <Loader2 className="h-8 w-8 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
        ) : (
          <Upload className="h-8 w-8 text-muted-foreground" />
        )}
        <div className="text-center">
          <p className="text-sm font-medium">CSV dosyasını sürükle ya da seç</p>
          <p className="mt-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            Yüklendikten sonra otomatik aktif batch olur.
          </p>
        </div>
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          size="sm"
          onClick={() => inputRef.current?.click()}
          disabled={busy}
        >
          Dosya Seç
        </Button>
        <input
          ref={inputRef}
          type="file"
          accept=".csv,text/csv"
          className="hidden"
          onChange={(e) => {
            const file = e.target.files?.[0];
            if (file) void handleFile(file);
            e.target.value = "";
          }}
        />
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}
```

---

# FILE: apps/web/src/features/import/ImportPage.tsx

```tsx
"use client";

import { useEffect, useRef } from "react";
import { usePathname, useRouter, useSearchParams } from "next/navigation";
import { BatchSelector } from "./BatchSelector";
import { ImportDropzone } from "./ImportDropzone";
import { useActiveBatch, useActivateBatch } from "./useBatch";

export function ImportPage() {
  const searchParams = useSearchParams();
  const router = useRouter();
  const pathname = usePathname();
  const active = useActiveBatch();
  const activate = useActivateBatch();
  const hydratedRef = useRef(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (hydratedRef.current) return;
    hydratedRef.current = true;
    const urlId = searchParams?.get("batch_id");
    if (!urlId) return;
    const numId = Number(urlId);
    if (!Number.isFinite(numId)) return;
    if (active.data && active.data.id === numId) return;
    activate.mutate(numId);
  }, [active.data, searchParams, activate]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const urlId = searchParams?.get("batch_id") ?? null;
    const activeId = active.data?.id != null ? String(active.data.id) : null;
    if (urlId === activeId) return;
    const url = activeId ? `${pathname}?batch_id=${activeId}` : pathname;
    router.replace(url, { scroll: false });
  }, [active.data, pathname, router, searchParams]);

  return (
    <main className="container mx-auto space-y-4 py-8">
      <header className="flex flex-col items-start gap-3 sm:flex-row sm:items-end sm:justify-between">
        <div>
          <p className="font-mono text-sm text-muted-foreground">MAGNA · Import</p>
          <h1 className="mt-1 text-3xl font-bold tracking-tight">CSV Import</h1>
        </div>
        <BatchSelector />
      </header>

      <ImportDropzone />
    </main>
  );
}
```

# FILE: apps/web/src/lib/api/client.ts (modify)

`delete` method eklendi:

```ts
/**
 * Tek tip API client (native fetch). Tüm FastAPI çağrıları buradan geçer.
 * Hata sözleşmesi: { error: { code, message, detail } } → ApiError'a çevrilir.
 */
import { env } from "@/lib/env";

export class ApiError extends Error {
  constructor(
    public readonly status: number,
    message: string,
    public readonly code?: string,
    public readonly detail?: unknown,
  ) {
    super(message);
    this.name = "ApiError";
  }
}

type RequestOptions = Omit<RequestInit, "body"> & { body?: unknown };

async function apiFetch<T>(path: string, options: RequestOptions = {}): Promise<T> {
  const { body, headers, ...rest } = options;
  const isForm = typeof FormData !== "undefined" && body instanceof FormData;

  const res = await fetch(`${env.apiUrl}${path}`, {
    ...rest,
    headers: isForm ? headers : { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...headers },
    body: body === undefined ? undefined : isForm ? (body as FormData) : JSON.stringify(body),
  });

  const isJson = res.headers.get("content-type")?.includes("application/json");
  const data = isJson ? await res.json() : await res.text();

  if (!res.ok) {
    const err = (data as { error?: { code?: string; message?: string; detail?: unknown } })?.error;
    throw new ApiError(res.status, err?.message ?? res.statusText, err?.code, err?.detail ?? data);
  }
  return data as T;
}

export const api = {
  get: <T>(path: string) => apiFetch<T>(path),
  post: <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) => apiFetch<T>(path, { method: "POST", body }),
  patch: <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) => apiFetch<T>(path, { method: "PATCH", body }),
  delete: <T = void>(path: string) => apiFetch<T>(path, { method: "DELETE" }),
  /** Multipart CSV yükleme — Content-Type'ı tarayıcı (boundary ile) ayarlar. */
  upload: <T>(path: string, form: FormData) => apiFetch<T>(path, { method: "POST", body: form }),
};
```

```ts
    detail: (id: number) => ["records", id] as const,

  validation: {

    summary: ["validation", "summary"] as const,

      ["analytics", "quality-distribution", filters] as const,
```

```tsx
export function Header() {

  const activeBatch = useActiveBatch();
  return (
    <header className="sticky top-0 z-30 border-b bg-card text-card-foreground">
      <div className="flex h-14 items-center gap-4 px-4">
        <Link href="/" className="flex shrink-0 items-baseline gap-2">
          <span className="font-mono text-xs text-muted-foreground">MAGNA</span>
          <span className="text-sm font-bold tracking-tight">Üretim Takip</span>
        </Link>

          {NAV_ITEMS.map((item) => {
            const isActive = isActivePath(item.href, pathname);
            return (
              <Link
                key={item.href}
                href={item.href}
                aria-current={isActive ? "page" : undefined}
                className={cn(
                  "shrink-0 rounded-md px-3 py-1.5 text-sm transition-colors",
                  isActive
                    ? "bg-primary text-primary-foreground"
                    : "text-foreground hover:bg-muted",
                )}
              >
                {item.label}
              </Link>
            );
          })}
        </nav>

        <div className="flex shrink-0 items-center gap-3">
          {activeBatch.data ? (
            <span className="hidden items-center gap-1.5 md:flex">
              <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Aktif:</span>
              <Badge tone="success" className="max-w-[180px] truncate">
                {activeBatch.data.filename}
              </Badge>
            </span>
          ) : null}
          <span className="hidden text-xs text-muted-foreground sm:inline">env:</span>
          <Badge tone="outline">development</Badge>
        </div>
      </div>
    </header>
  );
}
```

## Mimari Notlar

1. **Boundaries kuralı korunuyor:** `useActiveBatch` `src/hooks/` (shared) altında; Header (shared) doğrudan oradan okur. Feature kendi `useBatch.ts`'inde onu re-export eder — feature'ın public API'si eksiksiz kalır.

2. **`any` yasak:** Tüm generic parametreler ve response tipleri explicit; `api.delete<void>(...)` ile 204 için tip güvenliği.

3. **Tailwind token:** `bg-popover`, `bg-card`, `text-card-foreground`, `text-muted-foreground`, `border-input`, `border-primary`, `bg-accent`, `text-oee-good` — sadece semantic token.

4. **URL senkronu iki yönlü:** Mount'ta `?batch_id=N` farklıysa `activate(N)` çağrılır; aktif batch değişince `router.replace` ile URL senkronize olur. `hydratedRef` ile sonsuz döngü önlenir.

5. **Lightweight shadcn:** Popover/Command/AlertDialog Context-tabanlı, Radix yok; click-outside + Escape + ARIA rolleri dahil.

6. **Auto-activate:** Drag-drop başarılı → `mutateAsync(result.batch_id)` ile her zaman aktif olur (kullanıcı seçimini ezer — workflow: "bırak → çalışılan batch olur").

7. **AlertDialog onayı:** Her satırda Trash butonu → `confirmDelete` state → `AlertDialog` → `onConfirmDelete` → `useDeleteBatch.mutate`.

8. **Feature izolasyonu:** Diğer feature'lar import edilmez; `useActiveBatch` shared üzerinden paylaşılır.

Onay verirsen 14 dosyayı uygulayacağım. Devam edeyim mi?

Actually, the `React.cloneElement` signature for ref is special. The generic typing is:
```ts
function cloneElement<P>(
  element: ReactElement<P>,
  props?: Partial<P> & Attributes,

```

So `props` must be a partial of P (the original element's props). The ref prop in P is `Ref<HTMLButtonElement>` (from Button). When I provide `ref: (node: HTMLElement | null) => void`, this is a `RefCallback<HTMLElement>`, not matching `Ref<HTMLButtonElement>`.

In React's typing, `Ref<T>` = `RefCallback<T> | RefObject<T> | null`. So `RefCallback<HTMLElement>` is NOT a valid `Ref<HTMLButtonElement>`.

```tsx
  const ctx = usePopoverCtx();
```
```ts
  type ChildProps = {
    onClick?: (e: React.MouseEvent) => void;
```

```tsx
export function PopoverTrigger({ children, className }: PopoverTriggerProps) {
  const ctx = usePopoverCtx();
  type ChildProps = {
    onClick?: (e: React.MouseEvent) => void;
    ref?: React.Ref<HTMLElement>;
    className?: string;
  };
  const child = children as React.ReactElement<ChildProps>;
  const handleRef = (node: HTMLElement | null) => {
    ctx.triggerRef.current = node;
  };
  const handleClick = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    child.props.onClick?.(e);
    ctx.setOpen(!ctx.open);
  };
  const newProps = {
    onClick: handleClick,
    ref: handleRef,
    className: cn(child.props.className, className),
  };
  return React.cloneElement(child, newProps as Partial<ChildProps>);
}
```

The `as Partial<ChildProps>` should work since the newProps type is compatible. Let me think about this...

`handleRef` has type `(node: HTMLElement | null) => void`. This matches `RefCallback<HTMLElement>`, which is one of the `Ref<HTMLElement>` possibilities. So `handleRef` is assignable to `React.Ref<HTMLElement>`.

When cloneElement tries to apply `ref: Ref<HTMLElement>` to a Button (which expects `Ref<HTMLButtonElement>`), TypeScript will check if `Ref<HTMLElement>` is assignable to `Ref<HTMLButtonElement>`. Since `HTMLButtonElement extends HTMLElement`, a `Ref<HTMLButtonElement>` is more specific, and `Ref<HTMLElement>` is broader. 

For ref objects: `RefObject<HTMLElement>` is NOT assignable to `RefObject<HTMLButtonElement>` (RefObject is invariant in T because of the read-write `current`).

For ref callbacks: `RefCallback<HTMLElement>` (accepts HTMLElement) is assignable to `RefCallback<HTMLButtonElement>` (accepts HTMLButtonElement)? Wait, function parameters are contravariant. A callback that accepts HTMLElement can also accept HTMLButtonElement (since HTMLButtonElement is a subtype). So `RefCallback<HTMLElement>` is assignable to `RefCallback<HTMLButtonElement>`. Yes.

So if I make the ref a callback only, it should work. The TypeScript inference might be tricky though.

Let me just try it and see. If it fails, I'll add a type assertion.

Actually, let me check more carefully. `React.Ref<T>` = `RefCallback<T> | RefObject<T> | null | undefined`. When I assign a `RefCallback<HTMLElement>` to a slot expecting `Ref<HTMLButtonElement>`, TypeScript checks if `RefCallback<HTMLElement>` is assignable to `RefCallback<HTMLButtonElement> | RefObject<HTMLButtonElement> | null | undefined`. Since callbacks are contravariant, this is true: a function `(h: HTMLElement|null) => void` is assignable to `(b: HTMLButtonElement|null) => void` because the parameter type is wider.

So the ref assignment should work. Let me write the code:

```tsx
const handleRef: React.RefCallback<HTMLElement> = (node) => {
  ctx.triggerRef.current = node;
};
```

Hmm but `React.RefCallback<HTMLElement>` is `(instance: HTMLElement | null) => void | (() => void)`. The return type is `void | (() => void)`. My function returns `void` which is a subset. So it's assignable.

OK I think this should work. Let me just write the code and run typecheck.

Actually, I just realized — I can avoid the TS issue by using `useImperativeHandle` or by having PopoverTrigger not use cloneElement at all, just compose with Button.

Let me think practically: do I even NEED asChild? The only consumer is BatchSelector which uses a Button. I can have PopoverTrigger render a Button:

```tsx
export function PopoverTrigger({ children, className }: PopoverTriggerProps) {
  const ctx = usePopoverCtx();
  return (
    <Button
      variant="outline"
      onClick={() => ctx.setOpen(!ctx.open)}
      ref={(node) => {
        ctx.triggerRef.current = node;
      }}
      className={className}
    >
      {children}
    </Button>
  );
}
```

But this hardcodes `variant="outline"`. The consumer might want a different variant.

Hmm. Let me accept the ButtonProps:

```tsx
export type PopoverTriggerProps = ButtonProps & { children?: React.ReactNode };

export function PopoverTrigger({ children, className, ...buttonProps }: PopoverTriggerProps) {
  const ctx = usePopoverCtx();
  return (
    <Button
      {...buttonProps}
      onClick={(e) => {
        buttonProps.onClick?.(e);
        ctx.setOpen(!ctx.open);
      }}
      ref={(node) => {
        ctx.triggerRef.current = node;
      }}
      className={className}
    >
      {children}
    </Button>
  );
}
```

This works for BatchSelector. The consumer is:
```tsx
<PopoverTrigger className="w-[300px] justify-between gap-2">
  <span>...</span>
</PopoverTrigger>
```

But the consumer can't pass `variant` or `size` directly... unless I spread them:
```tsx
<PopoverTrigger variant="outline" size="default" className="...">
  ...
</PopoverTrigger>
```

OK this works. But it ties PopoverTrigger to Button. Not as flexible as shadcn's asChild, but for our use case it's fine.

```tsx
export type PopoverTriggerProps = ButtonProps;

export function PopoverTrigger({ children, className, ...buttonProps }: PopoverTriggerProps) {
  const ctx = usePopoverCtx();

      {...buttonProps}

      }}

}
```

OK let me proceed. Let me write all 14 files now.

Actually one more thing — for the type checking, let me think about the Popover trigger ref. I have:

```ts
triggerRef: React.MutableRefObject<HTMLElement | null>;
```

In `usePopoverCtx`, this is the type. In Popover, I create with `React.useRef<HTMLElement | null>(null)`. The type from useRef is `React.RefObject<HTMLElement | null>` (in React 19 it's slightly different, but generally).

`RefObject<T>` vs `MutableRefObject<T>`: RefObject is read-only (`{ readonly current: T | null }`), MutableRefObject is read-write. The context provides `MutableRefObject<HTMLElement | null>` because we need to assign to it. With `useRef<HTMLElement | null>(null)`, the type returned is `MutableRefObject<HTMLElement | null>` in React 18 (when initial value is not undefined). Good.

Now in the PopoverTrigger:
```tsx
ref={(node) => {
  ctx.triggerRef.current = node;
}}
```

This is a callback ref. The Button component's ref type is `Ref<HTMLButtonElement>` = `RefCallback<HTMLButtonElement> | RefObject<HTMLButtonElement> | null`. A callback `(node: HTMLButtonElement | null) => void` is `RefCallback<HTMLButtonElement>`. We're assigning to `ctx.triggerRef.current` which expects `HTMLElement | null`. `HTMLButtonElement` is a subtype of `HTMLElement`, so `HTMLButtonElement | null` is assignable to `HTMLElement | null`. ✓

OK the ref handling should work. Let me write the code.

For the existing lib files (query-keys.ts and api/client.ts), I need to edit them to add the new entries. Let me use Edit.

For the existing page.tsx and Header.tsx, I'll rewrite them with the new content using Write (since I already read them in this session).

**Key facts:**
1. **RecordFilter** doesn't have a `batch_id` field currently. The existing endpoints don't filter by `batch_id`.
2. The user wants `batch_id` as an **optional** query parameter for the 3 new endpoints.
3. The user said "mevcut endpoint'lere dokunma" — don't touch existing endpoints. So I should NOT add `batch_id` to the existing 5 endpoints. Only the 3 new ones get `batch_id`.
4. The `RecordFilter` model is shared. Adding `batch_id` to it would affect the existing filter behavior, but since I'm not touching existing endpoints, they wouldn't pass it. The `_apply_filter` function checks the field — if I add `batch_id` to `RecordFilter`, the existing filter function won't apply it (unless I also update `_apply_filter`). But the user said "mevcut endpoint'lere dokunma" — `_apply_filter` is in records/service.py, not analytics. Touching it would affect records endpoints too.

Two design choices:
- **A)** Add `batch_id` to `RecordFilter` schema + `_apply_filter`. The existing endpoints don't pass it, so they work unchanged. This is the cleanest.
- **B)** Don't touch `RecordFilter`. Add `batch_id` as a separate parameter to the 3 new service functions and apply it in their SQL directly.

Option A is cleaner (single source of truth for filter logic). Option B is more surgical (no impact on records).

- 3 new endpoints: each takes optional `batch_id: int | None = Query(None)`

### Detailed Schema Design:

**RecentRecordOut** — represents a single recent record. Based on the model:

```python
class RecentRecordOut(BaseModel):
    id: int
    prod_date: Optional[dt.date] = None
    shift: Optional[int] = None
    station_name: Optional[str] = None
    oee: Optional[float] = None
    status: str  # validation_status
    created_at: Optional[dt.datetime] = None
```

```python
class RecentRecordOut(BaseModel):
    id: int
    prod_date: Optional[dt.date] = None
    shift: Optional[int] = None
    station_name: Optional[str] = None
    stock_name: Optional[str] = None
    oee: Optional[float] = None
    produced_qty: Optional[int] = None
```

```python
class ProblemShiftOut(BaseModel):
```

### Limit and ordering:
- `recent_records`: limit by `LIMIT 20` (configurable?), ORDER BY `created_at DESC` or `prod_date DESC, id DESC`
- `top_stations`: limit by `LIMIT 10` (configurable?), ORDER BY `avg_oee DESC` or `total_production DESC`
- `problem_shifts`: limit? ORDER BY `avg_oee ASC` (worst first) or by `prod_date DESC`

### service.py — add 3 functions

```python
def recent_records(
    db: Session,
    batch_id: int | None = None,
    limit: int = 20,
) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
    stmt = select(
        models.ProductionRecord.id,
        models.ProductionRecord.prod_date,
        models.ProductionRecord.shift,
        models.ProductionRecord.station_name,
        models.ProductionRecord.stock_name,
        models.ProductionRecord.oee,
        models.ProductionRecord.produced_qty,
        models.ProductionRecord.scrap_qty,
        models.ProductionRecord.status,
        models.ProductionRecord.created_at,
    )
    if batch_id is not None:
        stmt = stmt.where(models.ProductionRecord.import_batch_id == batch_id)
    stmt = stmt.order_by(models.ProductionRecord.created_at.desc(), models.ProductionRecord.id.desc()).limit(limit)
    rows = db.execute(stmt).all()
    from app.features.analytics.schemas import RecentRecordOut
    return [
        RecentRecordOut(
            id=int(r.id),
            prod_date=r.prod_date,
            shift=int(r.shift) if r.shift is not None else None,
            station_name=r.station_name,
            stock_name=r.stock_name,
            oee=float(r.oee) if r.oee is not None else None,
            produced_qty=int(r.produced_qty) if r.produced_qty is not None else None,
            scrap_qty=int(r.scrap_qty) if r.scrap_qty is not None else None,
            status=str(r.status),
            created_at=r.created_at,
        ).model_dump()
        for r in rows
    ]


def top_stations(
    db: Session,
    batch_id: int | None = None,
    limit: int = 10,
) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
    stmt = (
        select(
            models.ProductionRecord.station_name.label("st"),
            func.avg(models.ProductionRecord.oee_recomputed).label("avg_oee"),
            func.coalesce(func.sum(models.ProductionRecord.produced_qty), 0).label("p"),
            func.coalesce(func.sum(models.ProductionRecord.scrap_qty), 0).label("sc"),
            func.count(models.ProductionRecord.id).label("cnt"),
        )
        .where(models.ProductionRecord.station_name.isnot(None))
        .group_by(models.ProductionRecord.station_name)
        .order_by(func.avg(models.ProductionRecord.oee_recomputed).desc())
        .limit(limit)
    )
    if batch_id is not None:
        stmt = stmt.where(models.ProductionRecord.import_batch_id == batch_id)
    rows = db.execute(stmt).all()
    from app.features.analytics.schemas import TopStationOut
    return [
        TopStationOut(
            station_name=str(r.st),
            avg_oee=float(r.avg_oee) if r.avg_oee is not None else None,
            total_production=int(r.p or 0),
            total_scrap=int(r.sc or 0),
            record_count=int(r.cnt or 0),
        ).model_dump()
        for r in rows
    ]


def problem_shifts(
    db: Session,
    batch_id: int | None = None,
    limit: int = 20,
) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
    avg_oee_col = func.avg(models.ProductionRecord.oee_recomputed).label("avg_oee")
    rejected_count = func.sum(
        case((models.ProductionRecord.status == "rejected", 1), else_=0)
    ).label("rejected_count")
    stmt = (
        select(
            models.ProductionRecord.prod_date.label("d"),
            models.ProductionRecord.shift.label("s"),
            models.ProductionRecord.station_name.label("st"),
            avg_oee_col,
            rejected_count,
            func.coalesce(func.sum(models.ProductionRecord.produced_qty), 0).label("p"),
            func.count(models.ProductionRecord.id).label("cnt"),
        )
        .where(models.ProductionRecord.shift.isnot(None))
        .group_by(
            models.ProductionRecord.prod_date,
            models.ProductionRecord.shift,
            models.ProductionRecord.station_name,
        )
        .having(
            or_(
                avg_oee_col < 60,
                rejected_count > 0,
            )
        )
        .order_by(avg_oee_col.asc())
        .limit(limit)
    )
    if batch_id is not None:
        stmt = stmt.where(models.ProductionRecord.import_batch_id == batch_id)
    rows = db.execute(stmt).all()
    from app.features.analytics.schemas import ProblemShiftOut
    return [
        ProblemShiftOut(
            prod_date=r.d,
            shift=int(r.s),
            station_name=r.st,
            avg_oee=float(r.avg_oee) if r.avg_oee is not None else None,
            rejected_count=int(r.rejected_count or 0),
            total_production=int(r.p or 0),
            record_count=int(r.cnt or 0),
        ).model_dump()
        for r in rows
    ]
```

Wait, there's an issue with `problem_shifts`. The `or_` and `case`/`func.sum` need to be imported. Let me check the existing imports:

```python
from sqlalchemy import case, func, select
```

I need to add `or_`. Let me also think about the having clause — it needs to reference the labels/columns properly.

Actually let me re-think. SQLAlchemy's `having` clause uses the column expressions. The `avg_oee_col` and `rejected_count` are the labeled columns. In HAVING, I can reference them by their label. But it's cleaner to compute the conditions inline:

```python
.having(
    or_(
        func.avg(models.ProductionRecord.oee_recomputed) < 60,
        func.sum(case((models.ProductionRecord.status == "rejected", 1), else_=0)) > 0,
    )
)
```

Or use the label and have MySQL/PostgreSQL accept it. SQLite (the project's DB) supports both. Let me use the label approach since it's cleaner.

Wait, I should also think about NULL values. If `oee_recomputed` is NULL for all records in a group, `AVG` is NULL. NULL < 60 is NULL (not TRUE), so the condition fails. The OR with `rejected_count > 0` might still match. So that's fine.

For `rejected_count`: the SUM might be 0 (if no rejected records in the group). 0 > 0 is FALSE. If there's at least one rejected, sum is >= 1, so > 0 is TRUE.

### api.py — add 3 endpoints

```python
@router.get("/recent-records")
def recent_records_endpoint(
    batch_id: Annotated[Optional[int], Query()] = None,
    limit: int = Query(20, ge=1, le=100),
    db: Session = Depends(get_db),
) -> list[dict[str, object]]:
    return recent_records(db, batch_id=batch_id, limit=limit)


@router.get("/top-stations")
def top_stations_endpoint(
    batch_id: Annotated[Optional[int], Query()] = None,
    limit: int = Query(10, ge=1, le=100),
    db: Session = Depends(get_db),
) -> list[dict[str, object]]:
    return top_stations(db, batch_id=batch_id, limit=limit)


@router.get("/problem-shifts")
def problem_shifts_endpoint(
    batch_id: Annotated[Optional[int], Query()] = None,
    limit: int = Query(20, ge=1, le=100),
    db: Session = Depends(get_db),
) -> list[dict[str, object]]:
    return problem_shifts(db, batch_id=batch_id, limit=limit)
```

# FILE: apps/api/app/features/analytics/schemas.py

```python
"""Analytics Pydantic şemaları."""
from __future__ import annotations

import datetime as dt
from typing import Optional

from pydantic import BaseModel


class KpiCards(BaseModel):
    avg_oee: Optional[float] = None
    total_production: int = 0
    total_scrap: int = 0
    total_down_time_minutes: float = 0.0
    record_count: int = 0
    valid_count: int = 0
    suspect_count: int = 0
    rejected_count: int = 0


class OeeTrendPoint(BaseModel):
    prod_date: dt.date
    avg_oee: Optional[float] = None
    total_production: int = 0
    record_count: int = 0


class ShiftComparisonRow(BaseModel):
    shift: int
    avg_oee: Optional[float] = None
    total_production: int = 0
    total_scrap: int = 0
    record_count: int = 0


class StationRankingRow(BaseModel):
    station_name: str
    avg_oee: Optional[float] = None
    total_production: int = 0
    record_count: int = 0


class QualityDistributionBucket(BaseModel):
    bucket_label: str
    bucket_start: float
    bucket_end: float
    record_count: int
    total_scrap: int = 0


class RecentRecordOut(BaseModel):
    id: int
    prod_date: Optional[dt.date] = None
    shift: Optional[int] = None
    station_name: Optional[str] = None
    stock_name: Optional[str] = None
    oee: Optional[float] = None
    produced_qty: Optional[int] = None
    scrap_qty: Optional[int] = None
    status: str
    created_at: Optional[dt.datetime] = None


class TopStationOut(BaseModel):
    station_name: str
    avg_oee: Optional[float] = None
    total_production: int = 0
    total_scrap: int = 0
    record_count: int = 0


class ProblemShiftOut(BaseModel):
    prod_date: Optional[dt.date] = None
    shift: int
    station_name: Optional[str] = None
    avg_oee: Optional[float] = None
    rejected_count: int = 0
    total_production: int = 0
    record_count: int = 0
```
